defined_text = {

	text = {
		trigger = {
			unique_missile_model_names = yes
		}

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { unique_missile_model_names = yes }
		}
		localization_key = missile_type_prod_10_selected_generic_loc
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GNSS_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^i > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^i }
				check_variable = { i = 0 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GNSS_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_yes
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^i > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^i } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { i = 0 } }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GNSS_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_no
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = total_sat_num_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:orbit_selected_TAG = {
				set_temp_variable = { temp1 = var_GNSS_sat_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = var_COM_sat_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = var_SPY_sat_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = var_KILL_sat_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = var_RODS_sat_total }
			}
		}
		localization_key = "[?temp1]"
	}
}

	name = TARGET_SAT_TAG_loc

		trigger = {
				set_temp_variable = { temp_target_TAG = ROOT.sat_target_array^i }
		}
		localization_key = TARGET_SAT_ID_loc_key
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GNSS1_model_sat_orbit_target_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { unique_missile_model_names_target_TAG = yes }
		}
		localization_key = missile_generic_ID_111_loc_key
	}

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ROOT.sat_target_TAG_array^i = USA.id }
		}

		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
